cakngd MkqeyL
(1871-1922)

À da kgnWgknWg ze LgEpy pgkze

oe nôLé zg nWgm iDahh
(MkgElèkg pakLlg)

Va RlXdlqLWèxeg édgnLkqhlxeg ze PeéXgn
vqddgnLlqh À Lqey dgy HghLy
fqdeEg 315 : Hgkylqh 1.6
2

vgLLg ézlLlqh heEéklyég kgpkghz dg LgJLg zg d’ézlLlqh
UaddlEakz, Makly, 1946-47, gh 15 HqdeEgy :
1. oe nôLé zg nWgm iDahh. MkgElèkg pakLlg.
2. oe nôLé zg nWgm iDahh. ogeJlèEg pakLlg.
3. À d’qEXkg zgy wgehgy Nlddgy gh Ndgeky. MkgElèkg pakLlg.
4. À d’qEXkg zgy wgehgy Nlddgy gh Ndgeky. ogeJlèEg pakLlg.
5. À d’qEXkg zgy wgehgy Nlddgy gh Ndgeky. BkqlylèEg pakLlg.
6. Vg nôLé zg UegkEahLgy. MkgElèkg pakLlg.
7. Vg nôLé zg UegkEahLgy. ogeJlèEg pakLlg.
8. Vg nôLé zg UegkEahLgy. BkqlylèEg pakLlg.
9. iqzqEg gL UqEqkkWg. MkgElèkg pakLlg.
10. iqzqEg gL UqEqkkWg. ogeJlèEg pakLlg.
11. Va Mklyqhhlèkg. MkgElèkg pakLlg.
12. Va Mklyqhhlèkg. ogeJlèEg pakLlg.
13. AdXgkLlhg zlypakeg.
14. Vg LgEpy kgLkqeHé. MkgElèkg pakLlg.
15. Vg LgEpy kgLkqeHé. ogeJlèEg pakLlg.

S
VqhYLgEpy, wg Eg yely nqenWé zg Xqhhg Wgekg.
MakNqly, à pglhg Ea XqeYlg éLglhLg, Egy jgeJ yg
NgkEalghL yl HlLg xeg wg h’aHaly pay dg LgEpy zg
Eg zlkg : « tg E’ghzqky. » OL, ehg zgEl-Wgekg
apkèy, da pghyég xe’ld éLalL LgEpy zg nWgknWgk dg
yqEEgld E’éHglddalL ; wg Hqedaly pqygk dg HqdeEg
xeg wg nkqjaly aHqlk zahy dgy Ealhy gL yqeNNdgk Ea
deElèkg ; wg h’aHaly pay ngyyé gh zqkEahL zg Nalkg
zgy kéNdgJlqhy yek ng xeg wg Hghaly zg dlkg, Ealy
ngy kéNdgJlqhy aHalghL pkly eh Lqek eh pge
pakLlnedlgk ; ld Eg ygEXdalL xeg w’éLaly Eql-EêEg
ng zqhL pakdalL d’qeHkaYg : ehg éYdlyg, eh xeaLeqk,
da klHadlLé zg Tkahçqly Sgk gL zg vWakdgy-PelhL.
vgLLg nkqjahng yekHlHalL pghzahL xegdxegy
ygnqhzgy à Eqh kéHgld ; gddg hg nWqxealL pay Ea
kalyqh, Ealy pgyalL nqEEg zgy énalddgy yek Egy
jgeJ gL dgy gEpênWalL zg yg kghzkg nqEpLg xeg dg
XqeYgqlk h’éLalL pdey addeEé. Mely gddg
nqEEghçalL à Eg zgHghlk lhlhLgddlYlXdg, nqEEg
7

apkèy da EéLgEpyjnqyg dgy pghyégy z’ehg
gJlyLghng ahLéklgekg ; dg yewgL ze dlHkg yg zéLanWalL
zg Eql, w’éLaly dlXkg zg E’j appdlxegk qe hqh ;
aeyylLôL wg kgnqeHkaly da Heg gL w’éLaly Xlgh éLqhhé
zg LkqeHgk aeLqek zg Eql ehg qXyneklLé, zqeng gL
kgpqyahLg pqek Egy jgeJ, Ealy pgeL-êLkg pdey
ghnqkg pqek Eqh gypklL, à xel gddg appakalyyalL
nqEEg ehg nWqyg yahy naeyg, lhnqEpkéWghylXdg,
nqEEg ehg nWqyg HkalEghL qXynekg. tg Eg
zgEahzaly xegddg Wgekg ld pqeHalL êLkg ;
w’ghLghzaly dg ylNNdgEghL zgy Lkalhy xel, pdey qe
Eqlhy édqlYhé, nqEEg dg nWahL z’eh qlygae zahy
ehg NqkêL, kgdgHahL dgy zlyLahngy, Eg zénklHalL
d’éLghzeg zg da naEpaYhg zéygkLg qù dg HqjaYgek
yg WâLg Hgky da yLaLlqh pkqnWalhg ; gL dg pgLlL
nWgElh xe’ld yelL Ha êLkg YkaHé zahy yqh yqeHghlk
pak d’gJnlLaLlqh xe’ld zqlL à zgy dlgeJ hqeHgaeJ, à
zgy anLgy lhannqeLeEéy, à da naeygklg kénghLg gL
aeJ azlgeJ yqey da daEpg éLkahYèkg xel dg yelHghL
ghnqkg zahy dg yldghng zg da helL, à da zqengek
pkqnWalhg ze kgLqek.
t’appejaly LghzkgEghL Egy wqegy nqhLkg dgy
Xgddgy wqegy zg d’qkglddgk xel, pdglhgy gL NkaînWgy,
yqhL nqEEg dgy wqegy zg hqLkg ghNahng. tg NkqLLaly
8

ehg addeEgLLg pqek kgYakzgk Ea EqhLkg. RlghLôL
ElhelL. v’gyL d’lhyLahL qù dg Eadazg, xel a éLé
qXdlYé zg pakLlk gh HqjaYg gL a zû nqenWgk zahy
eh WôLgd lhnqhhe, kéHglddé pak ehg nklyg, yg kéwqelL
gh apgkngHahL yqey da pqkLg ehg kalg zg wqek. Pegd
XqhWgek ! n’gyL zéwà dg EaLlh ! oahy eh EqEghL
dgy zqEgyLlxegy ygkqhL dgHéy, ld pqekka yqhhgk, qh
Hlghzka del pqkLgk ygnqeky. V’gypékahng z’êLkg
yqedaYé del zqhhg ze nqekaYg pqek yqeNNklk.
teyLgEghL ld a nke ghLghzkg zgy pay ; dgy pay yg
kappkqnWghL, pely y’édqlYhghL. OL da kalg zg wqek
xel éLalL yqey ya pqkLg a zlypake. v’gyL ElhelL ; qh
HlghL z’éLglhzkg dg Yam ; dg zgkhlgk zqEgyLlxeg gyL
pakLl gL ld Naezka kgyLgk LqeLg da helL à yqeNNklk yahy
kgEèzg.
tg Eg kghzqkEaly, gL pakNqly wg h’aHaly pdey
xeg zg nqekLy kéHgldy z’eh lhyLahL, dg LgEpy
z’ghLghzkg dgy nkaxegEghLy qkYahlxegy zgy
Xqlygklgy, z’qeHklk dgy jgeJ pqek NlJgk dg
Kadélzqynqpg zg d’qXyneklLé, zg YqûLgk Ykâng à ehg
degek EqEghLahég zg nqhynlghng dg yqEEgld qù
éLalghL pdqhYéy dgy EgeXdgy, da nWaEXkg, dg LqeL
zqhL wg h’éLaly xe’ehg pgLlLg pakLlg gL à
d’lhyghylXldlLé zexegd wg kgLqekhaly HlLg E’ehlk.
9

Ie Xlgh gh zqkEahL w’aHaly kgwqlhL yahy gNNqkL eh
âYg à waEaly kéHqde zg Ea Hlg pklElLlHg, kgLkqeHé
Lgddg zg Egy Lgkkgeky ghNahLlhgy nqEEg ngddg xeg
Eqh Ykahz-qhndg Eg LlkâL pak Egy Xqendgy gL
xe’aHalL zlyylpég dg wqek – zaLg pqek Eql z’ehg
èkg hqeHgddg – qù qh dgy aHalL nqepégy. t’aHaly
qeXdlé ngL éHéhgEghL pghzahL Eqh yqEEgld, w’gh
kgLkqeHaly dg yqeHghlk aeyylLôL xeg w’aHaly kéeyyl à
E’éHglddgk pqek énWappgk aeJ Ealhy zg Eqh
Ykahz-qhndg, Ealy pak Egyekg zg pkénaeLlqh
w’ghLqekaly nqEpdèLgEghL Ea LêLg zg Eqh qkglddgk
aHahL zg kgLqekhgk zahy dg Eqhzg zgy kêHgy.
PegdxegNqly, nqEEg ÈHg haxelL z’ehg nôLg
z’AzaE, ehg NgEEg halyyalL pghzahL Eqh
yqEEgld z’ehg Naeyyg pqylLlqh zg Ea nelyyg.
TqkEég ze pdalylk xeg w’éLaly yek dg pqlhL zg
YqûLgk, wg E’lEaYlhaly xeg n’éLalL gddg xel Eg
d’qNNkalL. cqh nqkpy xel yghLalL zahy dg ylgh Ea
pkqpkg nWadgek HqedalL y’j kgwqlhzkg, wg
E’éHglddaly. Vg kgyLg zgy WeEalhy E’appakalyyalL
nqEEg Xlgh dqlhLalh aepkèy zg ngLLg NgEEg xeg
w’aHaly xelLLég, ld j aHalL xegdxegy EqEghLy à
pglhg ; Ea wqeg éLalL nWaezg ghnqkg zg yqh Xalygk,
Eqh nqkpy nqekXaLeké pak dg pqlzy zg ya Lalddg. il,
10

nqEEg ld akklHalL xegdxegNqly, gddg aHalL dgy LkalLy
z’ehg NgEEg xeg w’aHaly nqhheg zahy da Hlg,
w’addaly Eg zqhhgk LqeL ghLlgk à ng XeL : da
kgLkqeHgk, nqEEg ngeJ xel pakLghL gh HqjaYg
pqek Hqlk zg dgeky jgeJ ehg nlLé zéylkég gL
y’lEaYlhghL xe’qh pgeL YqûLgk zahy ehg kéadlLé dg
nWakEg ze yqhYg. Mge à pge yqh yqeHghlk
y’éHahqelyyalL, w’aHaly qeXdlé da Nlddg zg Eqh kêHg.
sh WqEEg xel zqkL LlghL gh ngkndg aeLqek zg
del dg Nld zgy Wgekgy, d’qkzkg zgy ahhégy gL zgy
Eqhzgy. Sd dgy nqhyedLg z’lhyLlhnL gh y’éHglddahL,
gL j dlL gh ehg ygnqhzg dg pqlhL zg da Lgkkg xe’ld
qnnepg, dg LgEpy xel y’gyL énqedé weyxe’à yqh
kéHgld ; Ealy dgeky kahYy pgeHghL yg Eêdgk, yg
kqEpkg. Peg Hgky dg EaLlh apkèy xegdxeg
lhyqEhlg, dg yqEEgld dg pkghhg gh Lkalh zg dlkg,
zahy ehg pqyLekg Lkqp zlNNékghLg zg ngddg qù ld zqkL
WaXlLegddgEghL, ld yeNNlL zg yqh Xkay yqedgHé pqek
akkêLgk gL Nalkg kgnedgk dg yqdgld, gL à da pkgElèkg
ElheLg zg yqh kéHgld, ld hg yaeka pdey d’Wgekg, ld
gyLlEgka xe’ld HlghL à pglhg zg yg nqenWgk. Peg
y’ld y’ayyqeplL zahy ehg pqylLlqh ghnqkg pdey
zépdanég gL zlHgkYghLg, pak gJgEpdg apkèy zîhgk
ayyly zahy eh NaeLgeld, adqky dg XqedgHgkygEghL
11

ygka nqEpdgL zahy dgy Eqhzgy zéyqkXlLéy, dg
NaeLgeld EaYlxeg dg Ngka HqjaYgk à LqeLg HlLgyyg
zahy dg LgEpy gL zahy d’gypang, gL ae EqEghL
z’qeHklk dgy paeplèkgy, ld yg nkqlka nqenWé
xegdxegy Eqly pdey LôL zahy ehg aeLkg nqhLkég.
caly ld yeNNlyalL xeg, zahy Eqh dlL EêEg, Eqh
yqEEgld NûL pkqNqhz gL zéLghzîL ghLlèkgEghL Eqh
gypklL ; adqky ngdel-nl dânWalL dg pdah ze dlge qù wg
E’éLaly ghzqkEl, gL xeahz wg E’éHglddaly ae
Eldlge zg da helL, nqEEg w’lYhqkaly qù wg Eg
LkqeHaly, wg hg yaHaly EêEg pay ae pkgElgk
lhyLahL xel w’éLaly ; w’aHaly ygedgEghL zahy ya
ylEpdlnlLé pkgElèkg dg yghLlEghL zg d’gJlyLghng
nqEEg ld pgeL NkéElk ae Nqhz z’eh ahlEad ;
w’éLaly pdey zéheé xeg d’WqEEg zgy naHgkhgy ;
Ealy adqky dg yqeHghlk – hqh ghnqkg ze dlge qù
w’éLaly, Ealy zg xegdxegy-ehy zg ngeJ xeg w’aHaly
WaXlLéy gL qù w’aekaly pe êLkg – HghalL à Eql
nqEEg eh ygnqeky z’gh WaeL pqek Eg Llkgk ze
héahL z’qù wg h’aekaly pe yqkLlk LqeL yged ; wg
payyaly gh ehg ygnqhzg pak-zgyyey zgy ylèndgy zg
nlHldlyaLlqh, gL d’lEaYg nqhNeyéEghL ghLkgHeg zg
daEpgy à péLkqdg, pely zg nWgElygy à nqd kaXaLLe,
kgnqEpqyalL pge à pge dgy LkalLy qklYlhaeJ zg Eqh
12

Eql.
MgeL-êLkg d’lEEqXldlLé zgy nWqygy aeLqek zg
hqey dgek gyL-gddg lEpqyég pak hqLkg ngkLlLezg xeg
ng yqhL gddgy gL hqh pay z’aeLkgy, pak d’lEEqXldlLé
zg hqLkg pghyég gh Nang z’gddgy. Bqewqeky gyL-ld
xeg, xeahz wg Eg kéHglddaly alhyl, Eqh gypklL
y’aYlLahL pqek nWgknWgk, yahy j kéeyylk, à yaHqlk qù
w’éLaly, LqeL LqekhalL aeLqek zg Eql zahy
d’qXyneklLé, dgy nWqygy, dgy pajy, dgy ahhégy. cqh
nqkpy, Lkqp ghYqekzl pqek kgEegk, nWgknWalL,
z’apkèy da NqkEg zg ya NaLlYeg, à kgpékgk da
pqylLlqh zg ygy EgEXkgy pqek gh lhzelkg da
zlkgnLlqh ze Eek, da pdang zgy EgeXdgy, pqek
kgnqhyLkelkg gL pqek hqEEgk da zgEgekg qù ld yg
LkqeHalL. ia EéEqlkg, da EéEqlkg zg ygy nôLgy, zg
ygy YghqeJ, zg ygy épaedgy, del pkéyghLalL
yenngyylHgEghL pdeylgeky zgy nWaEXkgy qù ld aHalL
zqkEl, Lahzly xe’aeLqek zg del dgy Eeky lhHlylXdgy,
nWahYgahL zg pdang ygdqh da NqkEg zg da plèng
lEaYlhég, LqekXlddqhhalghL zahy dgy LéhèXkgy. OL
aHahL EêEg xeg Ea pghyég, xel WéylLalL ae ygeld
zgy LgEpy gL zgy NqkEgy, gûL lzghLlNlé dg dqYly gh
kappkqnWahL dgy nlknqhyLahngy, del, – Eqh nqkpy, –
yg kappgdalL pqek nWaneh dg Yghkg ze dlL, da pdang
13

zgy pqkLgy, da pklyg zg wqek zgy NghêLkgy,
d’gJlyLghng z’eh nqedqlk, aHgn da pghyég xeg
w’aHaly gh E’j ghzqkEahL gL xeg wg kgLkqeHaly ae
kéHgld. cqh nôLé ahKjdqyé, nWgknWahL à zgHlhgk
yqh qklghLaLlqh, y’lEaYlhalL, pak gJgEpdg, addqhYé
Nang ae Eek zahy eh Ykahz dlL à Xadzaxelh, gL
aeyylLôL wg Eg zlyaly : « Blghy, w’al Nlhl pak
E’ghzqkElk xeqlxeg EaEah hg yqlL pay Hgheg
Eg zlkg Xqhyqlk », w’éLaly à da naEpaYhg nWgm
Eqh Ykahz-pèkg, EqkL zgpely Xlgh zgy ahhégy ; gL
Eqh nqkpy, dg nôLé yek dgxegd wg Eg kgpqyaly,
Yakzlghy Nlzèdgy z’eh payyé xeg Eqh gypklL
h’aekalL waEaly zû qeXdlgk, Eg kappgdalghL da
NdaEEg zg da Hglddgeyg zg Hgkkg zg RqWêEg, gh
NqkEg z’ekhg, yeypghzeg ae pdaNqhz pak zgy
nWaîhgLLgy, da nWgElhég gh EakXkg zg ilghhg,
zahy Ea nWaEXkg à nqenWgk zg vqEXkaj, nWgm
Egy Ykahzy-pakghLy, gh zgy wqeky dqlhLalhy xe’gh
ng EqEghL wg Eg NlYekaly anLegdy yahy Eg dgy
kgpkéyghLgk gJanLgEghL, gL xeg wg kgHgkkaly ElgeJ
LqeL à d’Wgekg xeahz wg ygkaly LqeL à NalL éHglddé.
Mely kghalyyalL dg yqeHghlk z’ehg hqeHgddg
aLLlLezg ; dg Eek NldalL zahy ehg aeLkg zlkgnLlqh :
w’éLaly zahy Ea nWaEXkg nWgm c Eg zg ialhL-Vqep,
14

à da naEpaYhg. cqh olge ! Sd gyL ae Eqlhy zlJ
Wgekgy, qh zqlL aHqlk Nlhl zg zîhgk ! t’aekal Lkqp
pkqdqhYé da ylgyLg xeg wg Naly Lqey dgy yqlky gh
kghLkahL zg Ea pkqEghazg aHgn cEg zg ialhLVqep, aHahL z’ghzqyygk Eqh WaXlL. vak Xlgh zgy
ahhégy qhL payyé zgpely vqEXkaj, qù, zahy hqy
kgLqeky dgy pdey LakzlNy, n’éLalL dgy kgNdgLy kqeYgy
ze nqenWahL xeg wg Hqjaly yek dg HlLkaYg zg Ea
NghêLkg. v’gyL eh aeLkg Yghkg zg Hlg xe’qh Eèhg à
BahyqhHlddg, nWgm cEg zg ialhL-Vqep, eh aeLkg
Yghkg zg pdalylk xeg wg LkqeHg à hg yqkLlk xe’à da
helL, à yelHkg ae ndalk zg dehg ngy nWgElhy qù wg
wqealy wazly ae yqdgld ; gL da nWaEXkg qù wg Eg
ygkal ghzqkEl ae dlge zg E’WaXlddgk pqek dg zîhgk,
zg dqlh wg d’apgkçqly, xeahz hqey kghLkqhy,
LkaHgkyég pak dgy NgeJ zg da daEpg, yged pWakg
zahy da helL.
vgy éHqnaLlqhy LqekhqjahLgy gL nqhNeygy hg
zekalghL waEaly xeg xegdxegy ygnqhzgy ; yqeHghL,
Ea XkèHg lhngkLlLezg ze dlge qù wg Eg LkqeHaly hg
zlyLlhYealL pay ElgeJ dgy ehgy zgy aeLkgy dgy
zlHgkygy yeppqylLlqhy zqhL gddg éLalL NalLg, xeg
hqey h’lyqdqhy, gh HqjahL eh nWgHad nqeklk, dgy
pqylLlqhy yenngyylHgy xeg hqey EqhLkg dg
15

KlhéLqynqpg. caly w’aHaly kgHe LahLôL d’ehg, LahLôL
d’aeLkg, zgy nWaEXkgy xeg w’aHaly WaXlLégy zahy
Ea Hlg, gL wg Nlhlyyaly pak Eg dgy kappgdgk LqeLgy
zahy dgy dqhYegy kêHgklgy xel yelHalghL Eqh
kéHgld ; nWaEXkgy z’WlHgk qù xeahz qh gyL nqenWé,
qh yg XdqLLlL da LêLg zahy eh hlz xe’qh yg Lkgyyg
aHgn dgy nWqygy dgy pdey zlypakaLgy : eh nqlh zg
d’qkglddgk, dg WaeL zgy nqeHgkLekgy, eh XqeL zg
nWâdg, dg Xqkz ze dlL, gL eh heEékq zgy oéXaLy
kqygy, xe’qh NlhlL pak nlEghLgk ghygEXdg ygdqh da
LgnWhlxeg zgy qlygaeJ gh y’j appejahL
lhzéNlhlEghL ; qù, pak eh LgEpy Ydanlad, dg pdalylk
xe’qh YqûLg gyL zg yg yghLlk yépaké ze zgWqky
(nqEEg d’Wlkqhzgddg zg Egk xel a yqh hlz ae Nqhz
z’eh yqeLgkkalh zahy da nWadgek zg da Lgkkg), gL qù,
dg Nge éLahL ghLkgLghe LqeLg da helL zahy da
nWgElhég, qh zqkL zahy eh Ykahz EahLgae z’alk
nWaez gL NeEgeJ, LkaHgkyé zgy degeky zgy Llyqhy
xel yg kaddeEghL, yqkLg z’lEpadpaXdg adnôHg, zg
nWaezg naHgkhg nkgeyég ae yglh zg da nWaEXkg
EêEg, mqhg akzghLg gL EqXldg gh ygy nqhLqeky
LWgkElxegy, aékég zg yqeNNdgy xel hqey
kaNkaînWlyyghL da NlYekg gL HlghhghL zgy ahYdgy, zgy
pakLlgy Hqlylhgy zg da NghêLkg qe édqlYhégy ze
16

Nqjgk gL xel yg yqhL kgNkqlzlgy ; – nWaEXkgy z’éLé
qù d’qh alEg êLkg ehl à da helL Llèzg, qù dg ndalk zg
dehg appejé aeJ HqdgLy ghLk’qeHgkLy, wgLLg
weyxe’ae plgz ze dlL yqh énWgddg ghnWahLég, qù qh
zqkL pkgyxeg gh pdglh alk, nqEEg da EéyahYg
Xadahnég pak da Xklyg à da pqlhLg z’eh kajqh – ;
pakNqly da nWaEXkg Vqely CfS, yl Yalg xeg EêEg
dg pkgElgk yqlk wg h’j aHaly pay éLé Lkqp
EadWgekgeJ, gL qù dgy nqdqhhgLLgy xel yqeLghalghL
déYèkgEghL dg pdaNqhz y’énakLalghL aHgn LahL zg
Ykâng pqek EqhLkgk gL kéygkHgk da pdang ze dlL ;
pakNqly ae nqhLkalkg ngddg, pgLlLg gL yl édgHég zg
pdaNqhz, nkgeyég gh NqkEg zg pjkaElzg zahy da
WaeLgek zg zgeJ éLaYgy gL pakLlgddgEghL kgHêLeg
z’anawqe, qù, zèy da pkgElèkg ygnqhzg, w’aHaly éLé
lhLqJlxeé EqkadgEghL pak d’qzgek lhnqhheg ze
HéLlHgk, nqhHalhne zg d’WqyLldlLé zgy klzgaeJ
HlqdgLy gL zg d’lhyqdghLg lhzlNNékghng zg da pghzedg
xel wanayyalL LqeL WaeL nqEEg yl wg h’geyyg pay
éLé dà ; – qù ehg éLkahYg gL lEplLqjaXdg Ydang à
plgzy xeazkahYedalkgy XakkahL qXdlxegEghL eh zgy
ahYdgy zg da plèng yg nkgeyalL à HlN zahy da zqeng
pdéhlLezg zg Eqh nWaEp Hlyegd annqeLeEé eh
gEpdangEghL xel h’j éLalL pay pkéHe ; – qù Ea
17

pghyég, y’gNNqkçahL pghzahL zgy Wgekgy zg yg

d’WaXlLezg gL kézelL à ygy ygedy Eqjghy, ld ygkalL
lEpelyyahL à hqey kghzkg eh dqYly WaXlLaXdg.
vgkLgy, w’éLaly Xlgh éHglddé EalhLghahL : Eqh
nqkpy aHalL Hlké ehg zgkhlèkg Nqly gL dg Xqh ahYg
zg da ngkLlLezg aHalL LqeL akkêLé aeLqek zg Eql,
E’aHalL nqenWé yqey Egy nqeHgkLekgy, zahy Ea
nWaEXkg, gL aHalL Ely appkqJlEaLlHgEghL à dgek
18

pdang zahy d’qXyneklLé Ea nqEEqzg, Eqh Xekgae,
Ea nWgElhég, da NghêLkg yek da keg gL dgy zgeJ
pqkLgy. caly w’aHaly Xgae yaHqlk xeg wg h’éLaly pay
zahy dgy zgEgekgy zqhL d’lYhqkahng ze kéHgld

zlyLlhnLg, ze Eqlhy NalL nkqlkg da pkéyghng
pqyylXdg, dg Xkahdg éLalL zqhhé à Ea EéEqlkg ;
YéhékadgEghL wg hg nWgknWaly pay à Eg kghzqkElk
LqeL zg yelLg ; wg payyaly da pdey Ykahzg pakLlg zg
da helL à Eg kappgdgk hqLkg Hlg z’aeLkgNqly, à
vqEXkaj nWgm Ea Ykahz’LahLg, à RadXgn, à Makly,
à oqhnlèkgy, à fghlyg, alddgeky ghnqkg, à Eg
kappgdgk dgy dlgeJ, dgy pgkyqhhgy xeg w’j aHaly
nqhhegy, ng xeg w’aHaly He z’gddgy, ng xe’qh E’gh
aHalL kanqhLé.
À vqEXkaj, Lqey dgy wqeky zèy da Nlh zg
d’apkèy-Elzl, dqhYLgEpy aHahL dg EqEghL qù ld
NaezkalL Eg EgLLkg ae dlL gL kgyLgk, yahy zqkElk,
dqlh zg Ea Eèkg gL zg Ea Ykahz’Eèkg, Ea
nWaEXkg à nqenWgk kgzgHghalL dg pqlhL NlJg gL
zqedqekgeJ zg Egy pkéqnnepaLlqhy. Ih aHalL Xlgh
lhHghLé, pqek Eg zlyLkalkg dgy yqlky qù qh Eg
LkqeHalL d’alk Lkqp EadWgekgeJ, zg Eg zqhhgk ehg

dahLgkhg EaYlxeg, zqhL, gh aLLghzahL d’Wgekg ze

« nWadgL », qù wg Neyyg akklHé pqek da pkgElèkg Nqly

ahgyLWéylahLg

nqhhalyyalL Egy pakghLy gL dg XœeN à da nayygkqdg,

« n’gyL ehg plLlé zg kgyLgk ghNgkEé à da

xeg Hqey dg kghzkgm kqXeyLg gL éhgkYlxeg, zlyalLgddg LklyLgEghL, yekLqeL ng pgLlL xel a LahL Xgyqlh
zg pkghzkg zgy Nqkngy gL zg da HqdqhLé. » cqh

Ealy pay Lkqp NlJgEghL pqek hg pay nWgknWgk à

EqeHgEghLy zlHgky xe’gJnlLalghL zahy yqh âEg

yLeplzlLé zg Eqh ézenaLlqh gL da yjEéLklg zgy

zéygypqlk gL eh pkqXdèEg.

Peahz ngy Lqeky zg wakzlh zg Ea Ykahz’Eèkg
aHalghL dlge apkèy zîhgk, ehg nWqyg aHalL dg
pqeHqlk zg da Nalkg kghLkgk : n’éLalL, à eh zgy

gEpênWgk Lqh Eakl zg Xqlkg ze nqYhan ! » Mqek da
Laxelhgk, gh gNNgL (gddg aHalL appqkLé zahy da

YqeLLgy. ca paeHkg Ykahz’Eèkg ghLkalL, pklalL
akzgEEghL yqh Eakl zg hg pay YqûLgk ae nqYhan ;
ld yg NânWalL, XeHalL LqeL zg EêEg ya YqkYég, gL

yqeklahLg pqekLahL, nak gddg éLalL yl WeEXdg zg

z’WeEalhy, ld h’j aHalL z’lkqhlg xeg pqek gddgEêEg, gL pqek hqey Lqey nqEEg eh Xalygk zg ygy

26

zgWqky ghLkg dgy plgkkgy zg da Eekalddg gL xel

ghLk’qeHgkLg. ogyLlhég à eh eyaYg pdey ypénlad gL

pghzahL dg wqek weyxe’ae zqhwqh zg GqeyyalhHlddgdg-Mlh, ygkHlL dqhYLgEpy zg kgNeYg pqek Eql, yahy

pgkEly zg NgkEgk à ndgN, à LqeLgy ngddgy zg Egy
qnnepaLlqhy xel kéndaEalghL ehg lhHlqdaXdg
yqdlLezg : da dgnLekg, da kêHgklg, dgy dakEgy gL da
HqdepLé. Zéday ! wg hg yaHaly pay xeg, Xlgh pdey
LklyLgEghL xeg dgy pgLlLy énakLy zg kéYlEg zg yqh
Eakl, Eqh Eahxeg zg HqdqhLé, Ea yahLé zédlnaLg,
d’lhngkLlLezg xe’ldy pkqwgLalghL yek Eqh aHghlk,

zéaEXedaLlqhy lhngyyahLgy, zg d’apkèy-Elzl gL ze
yqlk, qù qh HqjalL payygk gL kgpayygk, qXdlxegEghL
dgHé Hgky dg nlgd, yqh Xgae HlyaYg aeJ wqegy
Xkehgy gL ylddqhhégy, zgHghegy ae kgLqek zg d’âYg
pkgyxeg EaeHgy nqEEg dgy daXqeky à d’aeLqEhg,

xegdxeg LklyLg pghyég, éLalL Lqewqeky gh Lkalh zg
yénWgk eh pdgek lhHqdqhLalkg.
27

ca ygedg nqhyqdaLlqh, xeahz wg EqhLaly Eg
nqenWgk, éLalL xeg EaEah HlghzkalL E’gEXkayygk

payyalL zahy dg nqedqlk à zqeXdg pqkLg dg XkelL
déYgk zg ya kqXg zg wakzlh gh Eqeyygdlhg Xdgeg, à
daxegddg pghzalghL zg pgLlLy nqkzqhy zg palddg

ahhqhçalL ngdel xel addalL dg yelHkg, qù gddg

dlLy zahy ya nWaEXkg, zly zqhn à Tkahçqlyg zg Lg

TazgLLg gL dgy caîLkgy iqhhgeky. ca Ykahz’Eèkg,

d’gypklL EêEg z’eh ghNahL ehg lhNdeghng pdey
zahYgkgeyg gL Eqlhy HlHlNlahLg xeg yek yqh nqkpy
dg Ykahz alk gL dg HghL ze dakYg. caly Eqh pèkg
d’ajahL pkgyxeg LkalLég zg Nqddg gh appkghahL dgy
dlHkgy xe’gddg HqedalL Eg zqhhgk, gddg éLalL
kgLqekhég gddg-EêEg à tqej-dg-flnqELg nWgm dg
dlXkalkg pqek xeg wg hg klyxeayyg pay zg hg pay
aHqlk Eqh nazgae (n’éLalL eh wqek XkûdahL gL gddg
éLalL kghLkég yl yqeNNkahLg xeg dg Eézgnlh aHalL
aHgkLl Ea Eèkg zg hg pay da dalyygk yg NaLlYegk
alhyl) gL gddg y’éLalL kaXaLLeg yek dgy xeaLkg kqEahy
nWaEpêLkgy zg UgqkYg iahz. « ca Nlddg, zlyalLgddg à EaEah, wg hg pqekkaly Eg zénlzgk à zqhhgk
à ngL ghNahL xegdxeg nWqyg zg Ead énklL. »
Oh kéadlLé, gddg hg yg kéylYhalL waEaly à klgh
anWgLgk zqhL qh hg pûL Llkgk eh pkqNlL lhLgddgnLegd,
gL yekLqeL ngdel xeg hqey pkqnekghL dgy Xgddgy
nWqygy gh hqey appkghahL à nWgknWgk hqLkg pdalylk
84

alddgeky xeg zahy dgy yaLlyNanLlqhy ze Xlgh-êLkg gL
zg da HahlLé. cêEg xeahz gddg aHalL à Nalkg à
xegdxe’eh eh nazgae zlL eLldg, xeahz gddg aHalL à
zqhhgk eh NaeLgeld, zgy nqeHgkLy, ehg nahhg, gddg
dgy nWgknWalL « ahnlghy », nqEEg yl dgek dqhYeg
zéyeéLezg ajahL gNNané dgek nakanLèkg z’eLldlLé, ldy
pakalyyalghL pdeLôL zlypqyéy pqek hqey kanqhLgk da
Hlg zgy WqEEgy z’aeLkgNqly xeg pqek ygkHlk aeJ
Xgyqlhy zg da hôLkg. Oddg gûL alEé xeg w’geyyg
zahy Ea nWaEXkg zgy pWqLqYkapWlgy zgy
EqheEghLy qe zgy pajyaYgy dgy pdey XgaeJ. caly
ae EqEghL z’gh Nalkg d’gEpdgLLg, gL Xlgh xeg da
nWqyg kgpkéyghLég gûL ehg Hadgek gyLWéLlxeg, gddg
LkqeHalL xeg da HedYaklLé, d’eLldlLé kgpkghalghL Lkqp
HlLg dgek pdang zahy dg Eqzg Eénahlxeg zg
kgpkéyghLaLlqh, da pWqLqYkapWlg. Oddg gyyajalL zg
keygk gL, ylhqh z’édlElhgk ghLlèkgEghL da XahadlLé
nqEEgknladg, ze Eqlhy zg da kézelkg, z’j
yeXyLlLegk, pqek da pdey Ykahzg pakLlg, zg d’akL
ghnqkg, z’j lhLkqzelkg nqEEg pdeylgeky
« épalyygeky » z’akL : ae dlge zg pWqLqYkapWlgy zg
da vaLWézkadg zg vWakLkgy, zgy Ukahzgy OaeJ zg
ialhL-vdqez, ze féyeHg, gddg yg kghyglYhalL

aHalL pay kgpkéyghLéy, gL pkéNékalL Eg zqhhgk zgy
pWqLqYkapWlgy zg da vaLWézkadg zg vWakLkgy pak
vqkqL, zgy Ukahzgy OaeJ zg ialhL-vdqez pak
ZeXgkL GqXgkL, ze féyeHg pak Bekhgk, ng xel
NalyalL eh zgYké z’akL zg pdey. caly yl dg
pWqLqYkapWg aHalL éLé énakLé zg da kgpkéyghLaLlqh
ze nWgN-z’œeHkg qe zg da haLekg gL kgEpdané pak
eh Ykahz akLlyLg, ld kgpkghalL ygy zkqlLy pqek
kgpkqzelkg ngLLg lhLgkpkéLaLlqh EêEg. AkklHég à

zahy eh éLaL qù hqey hg pqeHqhy pdey dg Hqlk
aewqekz’Wel (nqEEg da YkaHekg zg da vèhg zg
Véqhakz aHahL ya zéYkazaLlqh, pak cqkYah). Sd
NaeL zlkg xeg dgy kéyedLaLy zg ngLLg Eahlèkg zg

zqhhég zg ylEpdgy pWqLqYkapWlgy. Ih hg pqeHalL

aLLaxegk zahy dg Lqh xe’ld NaeL d’annghL nqkzlad xel

v’gyL alhyl xeg, pghzahL dqhYLgEpy, xeahz,

HgyLlXedg qù wg E’anWgElhaly Hgky da pkgElèkg
EaknWg zg d’gynadlgk, yl nkegd à EqhLgk, xel
nqhyLlLealL à del yged dg Lkqhn NqkL éLkqlL zg ngLLg
pjkaElzg lkkéYedlèkg ; gL, ae NaîLg, Ea nWaEXkg à
nqenWgk aHgn dg pgLlL nqedqlk à pqkLg HlLkég pqek
d’ghLkég zg EaEah ; gh eh EqL, Lqewqeky He à da
EêEg Wgekg, lyqdé zg LqeL ng xe’ld pqeHalL j aHqlk
aeLqek, yg zéLanWahL yged yek d’qXyneklLé, dg zénqk
yLklnLgEghL héngyyalkg (nqEEg ngdel xe’qh HqlL
lhzlxeé gh LêLg zgy Hlglddgy plèngy pqek dgy
kgpkéyghLaLlqhy gh pkqHlhng) ae zkaEg zg Eqh
zéyWaXlddaYg ; nqEEg yl vqEXkaj h’aHalL
nqhylyLé xe’gh zgeJ éLaYgy kgdléy pak eh Elhng
gynadlgk gL nqEEg y’ld h’j aHalL waEaly éLé xeg
ygpL Wgekgy ze yqlk. À Hkal zlkg, w’aekaly pe
képqhzkg à xel E’gûL lhLgkkqYé xeg vqEXkaj
nqEpkghalL ghnqkg aeLkg nWqyg gL gJlyLalL à
z’aeLkgy Wgekgy. caly nqEEg ng xeg wg E’gh
ygkaly kappgdé E’gûL éLé Nqekhl ygedgEghL pak da
EéEqlkg HqdqhLalkg, da EéEqlkg zg d’lhLgddlYghng,
gL nqEEg dgy kghyglYhgEghLy xe’gddg zqhhg yek dg
payyé hg nqhygkHghL klgh zg del, wg h’aekaly waEaly
ge ghHlg zg yqhYgk à ng kgyLg zg vqEXkaj. BqeL
ngda éLalL gh kéadlLé EqkL pqek Eql.

cqkL à waEaly ? v’éLalL pqyylXdg.
Sd j a Xgaenqep zg Wayakz gh LqeL ngnl, gL eh
ygnqhz Wayakz, ngdel zg hqLkg EqkL, yqeHghL hg
hqey pgkEgL pay z’aLLghzkg dqhYLgEpy dgy NaHgeky
ze pkgElgk.
tg LkqeHg Lkèy kalyqhhaXdg da nkqjahng ngdLlxeg
xeg dgy âEgy zg ngeJ xeg hqey aHqhy pgkzey yqhL
napLlHgy zahy xegdxeg êLkg lhNéklgek, zahy ehg

gNNgL pqek hqey weyxe’ae wqek, xel pqek Xgaenqep
hg HlghL waEaly, qù hqey hqey LkqeHqhy payygk
pkèy zg d’akXkg, ghLkgk gh pqyygyylqh zg d’qXwgL xel
gyL dgek pklyqh. Adqky gddgy LkgyyalddghL, hqey
appgddghL, gL ylLôL xeg hqey dgy aHqhy kgnqhhegy,
d’ghnWahLgEghL gyL Xklyé. oédlHkégy pak hqey,
gddgy qhL Halhne da EqkL gL kgHlghhghL HlHkg aHgn
hqey.
Sd gh gyL alhyl zg hqLkg payyé. v’gyL pglhg
pgkzeg xeg hqey nWgknWlqhy à d’éHqxegk, Lqey dgy
gNNqkLy zg hqLkg lhLgddlYghng yqhL lheLldgy. Sd gyL
nanWé Wqky zg yqh zqEalhg gL zg ya pqkLég, gh
xegdxeg qXwgL EaLéklgd (gh da yghyaLlqh xeg hqey
zqhhgkalL ngL qXwgL EaLéklgd), xeg hqey hg
94

yqepçqhhqhy pay. vgL qXwgL, ld zépghz ze Wayakz
xeg hqey dg kghnqhLklqhy aHahL zg Eqeklk, qe xeg
hqey hg dg kghnqhLklqhy pay.
Sd j aHalL zéwà Xlgh zgy ahhégy xeg, zg
vqEXkaj, LqeL ng xel h’éLalL pay dg LWéâLkg gL dg
zkaEg zg Eqh nqenWgk h’gJlyLalL pdey pqek Eql,
xeahz eh wqek z’WlHgk, nqEEg wg kghLkaly à da
Ealyqh, Ea Eèkg, HqjahL xeg w’aHaly Nkqlz, Eg
pkqpqya zg Eg Nalkg pkghzkg, nqhLkg Eqh
WaXlLezg, eh pge zg LWé. tg kgNeyal z’aXqkz gL, wg
hg yaly pqekxeql, Eg kaHlyal. Oddg ghHqja
nWgknWgk eh zg ngy YâLgaeJ nqekLy gL zqzey
appgdéy MgLlLgy cazgdglhgy xel ygEXdghL aHqlk éLé
Eqedéy zahy da HadHg kalhekég z’ehg nqxelddg zg
ialhL-tanxegy. OL XlghLôL, EanWlhadgEghL,

hqey YaYhlqhy hqy nWalygy, nqEEg zahy ehg

yglh z’eh pajy akkqyé z’gaeJ HlHgy, Hqey
E’éHqxegm ghnqkg ngLLg Hlg xeahz wg pghyg à Hqey
gL Hqey da nqhLghgm gh gNNgL pqek d’aHqlk pge à pge
nqhLqekhég gL ghndqyg – Lahzly xeg wg pkqYkgyyaly
zahy Ea dgnLekg gL xeg LqEXalL da nWadgek ze wqek
– zahy dg nklyLad yenngyylN, dghLgEghL nWahYgahL gL
LkaHgkyé zg NgelddaYgy, zg Hqy Wgekgy yldghnlgeygy,
yqhqkgy, qzqkahLgy gL dlEplzgy.
186

PegdxegNqly w’éLaly Llké zg Ea dgnLekg, zèy dg
Eldlge zg d’apkèy-Elzl, pak da Nlddg ze wakzlhlgk,

payyaYg eh qkahYgk, yg nqepahL eh zqlYL, yg
nayyahL ehg zghL gL nklahL : « Vgy Hqldà, dgy
Hqldà ! » pqek xeg Tkahçqlyg gL Eql hqey
annqeklqhy gL hg Eahxelqhy klgh ze ypgnLandg.
v’éLalL dgy wqeky qù, pqek zgy EahœeHkgy zg
Yakhlyqh, da Lkqepg LkaHgkyalL vqEXkaj, pkghahL
YéhékadgEghL da keg ialhLg-ZldzgYakzg. Bahzly
xeg hqy zqEgyLlxegy ayyly gh kahY yek zgy nWalygy

zqElhlnaeJ zg vqEXkaj gL yg NalyalghL Hqlk

dalyyalghL ghLkg gddgy zgeJ Ealyqhy dqlhLalhgy zg
d’aHgheg zg da Uakg, aHalL apgkçe d’éndaL zgy
nayxegy. Vgy zqEgyLlxegy aHalghL kghLké
pkénlplLaEEghL dgeky nWalygy, nak xeahz dgy
nelkayylgky zéNldalghL keg ialhLg-ZldzgYakzg, ldy gh

nWgHaeJ kayalL dgy Ealyqhy, nqeHkahL dgy LkqLLqlky
yeXEgkYéy nqEEg zgy XgkYgy xel qNNkghL eh dlL
Lkqp éLkqlL à eh LqkkghL zénWaîhé.
– MaeHkgy ghNahLy, zlyalL Tkahçqlyg à pglhg

akklHég à da Yklddg gL zéwà gh dakEgy ; paeHkg

zg Hqlk zgy wgehgy Yghy xel hg LlghhghL pay à da

– og hg pay Lghlk à da Hlg ? caly à xeql zqhn
xe’ld NaeL Lghlk, yl ng h’gyL pay à da Hlg, dg yged
nazgae xeg dg Xqh olge hg Nayyg waEaly zgeJ Nqly.

LlghhghL pay ! tg dgy al Hey gh 70 ; ldy h’qhL pdey
pgek zg da EqkL, zahy ngy ElyékaXdgy Yegkkgy ;

HadghL pdey da nqkzg pqek dgy pghzkg, ng h’gyL pay
zgy WqEEgy, n’gyL zgy dlqhy. (Mqek Tkahçqlyg da
nqEpakalyqh z’eh WqEEg à eh dlqh, xe’gddg
pkqhqhçalL dl-qh, h’aHalL klgh zg NdaLLgek.)

da Yakg xe’qh apgkngHalL Lqewqeky zg hqeHgaeJ

– fqjgm-Hqey, Tkahçqlyg, zlyalL dg wakzlhlgk, da

HqhL.

pdey Nkahn.

ylYhlNlalghL klgh ze LqeL. RdqnW gh gNNgL hg NeL pay

LadlE), Ealy w’aHaly pgek xeg Eqh naEakazg hg dg
nqhhûL gL hg kéLaXdîL dgy pakqdgy.

xel d’éLalghL gh gNNgL, Ealy EêEg ng xe’ld j aHalL
xegdxegNqly zg NânWgeJ zahy dgek NaElddg.
– OL nqEEghL y’appgddg-L-ld Lqh aEl xel HlghL
ng yqlk ?

v’gyL eh lEXénldg.

zlL-gddg, pelyxe’ld hg Eg nqhhaîL pay ; qe Xlgh

zg Ea Ykahz’Eèkg h’éLalghL pay NglhLgy ; Ealy ldy
yaHalghL z’lhyLlhnL qe pak gJpéklghng xeg dgy

gJlYghngy zg d’aElLlé yek eh ylEpdg EqeHgEghL
zg dgek lEaYlhaLlqh gL zg dgek yghylXldlLé, hg da

xe’gddgy hqey zqlHghL ngy haLekgy zqhL Ea

pakdalL waEaly, hg EqzlNla pay pqek ngda dg
LgyLaEghL qù gddg del dalyyalL LqeLg ya NqkLehg,

caly w’alEaly RdqnW, Egy pakghLy HqedalghL Eg

weYgâL pgkhlnlgeygy. OL qh d’aekalL ghnqkg kgçe à

E’appkghzkg – hqeHgddg xel pdey Lakz geL

Wgekgeyg, pely pdey EadWgekgeyg – xeg LqeLgy dgy
NgEEgy hg pghyalghL xe’à d’aEqek gL xe’ld h’j gh
a pay zqhL qh hg pûL Halhnkg dgy kéylyLahngy, ld hg
E’aHalL ayyeké aHqlk ghLghze zlkg zg da Naçqh da
pdey ngkLalhg xeg Ea Ykahz’LahLg aHalL ge ehg

NeL gJLkêEgEghL Nkqlz pqek Eql.
caly ae yewgL zg RgkYqLLg ld aHalL zlL Hkal.

Ykahz’Eèkg – xeg hqey h’gh aeklqhy pay pkqNlLé.

Qqey kghLklqhy Lqewqeky zg Xqhhg Wgekg zg hqy
pkqEghazgy pqek pqeHqlk Nalkg ehg HlylLg à Ea

éLalL yqeHghL ngkLlNlég pak xegdxeg Nlddg zgy

pak ehg nqhNkqhLaLlqh aHgn da haLekg, zg weYgk zg

zahy dgy Eeky zexegd wg h’al waEaly péhéLké,

ngyyé pqek hqey, nqhLlhealL à êLkg nWâLlé nqEEg
eh HlddaYg zg da RlXdg pak LqeLgy dgy dahngy zg
d’qkaYg xel NdaYgddalghL qXdlxegEghL dgy zgEgekgy

olge dg Mèkg xel NalyalL zgynghzkg Hgky del,

qyLghyqlk z’aeLgd, dgy LlYgy z’qk gNNkahYégy zg yqh
yqdgld kgpake.

xe’ldy pkqEgLLalghL zg zgEgekgk dà, nqEEg zgy

flhLgeld, z’eh alk day, YaenWg, aNNalké, WqhhêLg gL

yaHaly EalhLghahL, pqek LqeLgy dgy yqeNNkahngy
xeg pghzahL ya Hlg c. flhLgeld aHalL yeppqkLégy à
naeyg zg ya Nlddg, ng xe’apkèy da EqkL ld aHalL kgçe
z’gddg gh yadalkg.
OL pqekLahL w’al pghyé zgpely xeg yl c.
flhLgeld aHalL pe ayylyLgk à ngLLg ynèhg, ld h’gûL
pgeL-êLkg pay ghnqkg pgkze ya Nql zahy dg Xqh
nœek zg ya Nlddg, gL pgeL-êLkg EêEg h’gûL-ld pay ge
gh ngda LqeL à NalL LqkL. vgkLgy, zahy dgy WaXlLezgy
zg cddg flhLgeld d’appakghng ze Ead éLalL yl ghLlèkg
xe’qh aekalL ge zg da pglhg à da kghnqhLkgk kéadlyég
à ng zgYké zg pgkNgnLlqh alddgeky xeg nWgm ehg
yazlxeg ; n’gyL à da deElèkg zg da kaEpg zgy

z’ehg Ealyqh zg naEpaYhg HéklLaXdg xe’qh pgeL

aekalL pgeL-êLkg zgy EahxegEghLy aeyyl nkegdy

lEpkgyylqhy zg NqkEg, zg pakNeE qe zg nqedgek –
zg LânWgk z’apgkngHqlk ng xel yg nanWalL zgkklèkg
gddgy, xeg wg hg Lakzaly pay à Eg nWgknWgk à EqlEêEg zgy gJneygy xel Eg pgkElyyghL zg Eg
zékqXgk à ngy gNNqkLy gL zg E’épakYhgk ngLLg
NaLlYeg. Mak XqhWgek Egy pakghLy E’appgdalghL, wg
yghLaly xeg wg h’aHaly pay pkéyghLgEghL da
LkahxelddlLé héngyyalkg pqek pqekyelHkg eLldgEghL
Ea kgnWgknWg, gL xe’ld HadalL ElgeJ h’j pdey
pghygk weyxe’à ng xeg wg Neyyg kghLké, gL hg pay Eg
379

NaLlYegk z’aHahng yahy kéyedLaL. Adqky wg hg
E’qnnepaly pdey zg ngLLg nWqyg lhnqhheg xel
y’ghHgdqppalL z’ehg NqkEg qe z’eh pakNeE, Xlgh
Lkahxelddg pelyxeg wg da kaEghaly à da Ealyqh,
pkqLéYég pak dg kgHêLgEghL z’lEaYgy yqey
dgyxegddgy wg da LkqeHgkaly HlHahLg, nqEEg dgy
pqlyyqhy xeg, dgy wqeky qù qh E’aHalL dalyyé addgk à
da pênWg, wg kappqkLaly zahy Eqh pahlgk, nqeHgkLy
pak ehg nqenWg z’WgkXg xel pkéygkHalL dgek
NkaînWgek. shg Nqly à da Ealyqh wg yqhYgaly à aeLkg
nWqyg gL alhyl y’ghLayyalghL zahy Eqh gypklL
(nqEEg zahy Ea nWaEXkg dgy Ndgeky xeg w’aHaly
neglddlgy zahy Egy pkqEghazgy qe dgy qXwgLy
xe’qh E’aHalL zqhhéy), ehg plgkkg qù wqealL eh
kgNdgL, eh LqlL, eh yqh zg ndqnWg, ehg qzgek zg
Ngelddgy, Xlgh zgy lEaYgy zlNNékghLgy yqey
dgyxegddgy ld j a dqhYLgEpy xe’gyL EqkLg da kéadlLé
pkgyyghLlg xeg wg h’al pay ge ayygm zg HqdqhLé
pqek akklHgk à zénqeHklk. shg Nqly pqekLahL – qù
hqLkg pkqEghazg y’éLahL pkqdqhYég NqkL ae zgdà zg
ya zekég WaXlLegddg, hqey aHlqhy éLé Xlgh WgekgeJ
zg kghnqhLkgk à El-nWgElh ze kgLqek, nqEEg
d’apkèy-Elzl NlhlyyalL, dg zqnLgek Mgkngplgz xel
payyalL gh HqlLekg à Xklzg aXaLLeg, hqey aHalL

kgnqhhey gL NalL EqhLgk aHgn del – w’gey ehg
lEpkgyylqh zg ng Yghkg gL hg d’aXahzqhhal pay
yahy eh pge d’appkqNqhzlk. Ih E’aHalL NalL EqhLgk
pkèy ze nqnWgk, hqey addlqhy nqEEg dg HghL pakng
xeg dg zqnLgek aHalL ghnqkg aHahL zg kghLkgk à
vqEXkaj à y’akkêLgk à cakLlhHlddg-dg-ign nWgm eh
Eadazg à da pqkLg zexegd ld aHalL éLé nqhHghe xeg
hqey d’aLLghzklqhy. Ae LqekhahL z’eh nWgElh
w’épkqeHal LqeL à nqep ng pdalylk ypénlad xel hg
kgyygEXdalL à aeneh aeLkg, à apgkngHqlk dgy zgeJ
ndqnWgky zg cakLlhHlddg, yek dgyxegdy zqhhalL dg
yqdgld nqenWahL gL xeg dg EqeHgEghL zg hqLkg
HqlLekg gL dgy dangLy ze nWgElh aHalghL d’alk zg
Nalkg nWahYgk zg pdang, pely ngdel zg flgeJHlnx
xel, yépaké z’geJ pak ehg nqddlhg gL ehg Haddég, gL
ylLeé yek eh pdaLgae pdey édgHé zahy dg dqlhLalh,
ygEXdalL pqekLahL LqeL Hqlylh z’geJ.
Oh nqhyLaLahL, gh hqLahL da NqkEg zg dgek
NdènWg, dg zépdangEghL zg dgeky dlYhgy,
d’ghyqdglddgEghL zg dgek yekNang, wg yghLaly xeg wg
h’addaly pay ae XqeL zg Eqh lEpkgyylqh, xeg
xegdxeg nWqyg éLalL zgkklèkg ng EqeHgEghL,
zgkklèkg ngLLg ndakLé, xegdxeg nWqyg xe’ldy
ygEXdalghL nqhLghlk gL zékqXgk à da Nqly.

Vgy ndqnWgky pakalyyalghL yl édqlYhéy gL hqey
aHlqhy d’alk zg yl pge hqey kappkqnWgk z’geJ, xeg

kappgdgk Egy ndqnWgky. RlghLôL, dgeky dlYhgy gL
dgeky yekNangy ghyqdglddégy, nqEEg yl gddgy aHalghL

ge à Nalkg yeXlk xeg pge zg nWahYgEghLy :
« igedy, y’édgHahL ze hlHgae zg da pdalhg gL

« tg hg kgpghyal waEaly à ngLLg paYg, Ealy à ng

Xeddg NqkEég nqhLkg ehg pdahLg axeaLlxeg pak
d’gae zg da klHlèkg gL xel nkèHg aeyylLôL, Eqh
gJadLaLlqh dgy a pqkLéy gL a kéeyyl à dgek Nalkg

xe’adghLqek dgy nWgElhy yg yqhL gNNanéy gL xeg

ngeJ xel dgy NqedèkghL. MakNqly ng Eqkngae zg
pajyaYg aEghé alhyl weyxe’à aewqekz’Wel yg
zéLanWg yl lyqdé zg LqeL, xe’ld NdqLLg lhngkLalh zahy
Ea pghyég nqEEg ehg oédqy Ndgeklg, yahy xeg wg
pelyyg zlkg zg xegd pajy, zg xegd LgEpy – pgeLêLkg LqeL ylEpdgEghL zg xegd kêHg – ld HlghL. caly
n’gyL yekLqeL nqEEg à zgy YlygEghLy pkqNqhzy zg

dgyxegdy wg E’appelg ghnqkg, xeg wg zqly pghygk

aEl qe aHgn ya EaîLkgyyg. oahy dg nay nqhLkalkg,

kanqhLa à c. fgkzeklh xe’gddg aHalL NalL da
nqhhalyyahng z’eh WqEEg nWakEahL, c. iDahh,
gL lhylhea xe’ld ygkalL Lkèy WgekgeJ z’êLkg kgçe
nWgm geJ, c. fgkzeklh LkahyElL-ld yéahng LghahLg
da kgxeêLg à ya NgEEg. (Sd h’aHalL waEaly z’aHly
xe’apkèy ya NgEEg, zqhL yqh kôdg pakLlnedlgk éLalL

z’lhYéhlqylLé.)

eh hqeHgd aEqek.
